 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right">Exhibit 99.1 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:13pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT
 COLOR="#666666">Microsoft Cloud Growth Fuels Second Quarter Results </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><I>Results include a net charge of $13.8&nbsp;billion related to
the Tax Cuts and Jobs Act </I></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>REDMOND, Wash. &#151; January</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;31, 2018 &#151; </B>Microsoft Corp. today announced
the following results for the quarter ended December&nbsp;31, 2017: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Revenue was $28.9&nbsp;billion and increased 12% </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Operating income was $8.7&nbsp;billion and increased 10% </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">GAAP net loss was $(6.3) billion and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> net income was $7.5&nbsp;billion </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">GAAP diluted loss per share was $(0.82) and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> diluted earnings per share was $0.96 </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">GAAP results include a $13.8&nbsp;billion net charge related to the Tax Cuts and Jobs Act (TCJA) </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#147;This quarter&#146;s results speak to the differentiated value we are delivering to customers across our productivity solutions and as the
hybrid cloud provider of choice,&#148; said Satya Nadella, chief executive officer of Microsoft. &#147;Our investments in IoT, data, and AI services across cloud and the edge position us to further accelerate growth.&#148; </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">The following table reconciles our financial results reported in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles (GAAP) to <FONT

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Satya Nadella, chief executive officer, Amy Hood, executive vice president and chief financial officer, Frank Brod, chief accounting officer,

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><I>TCJA Impact.</I> We recorded a net charge of $13.8&nbsp;billion related to TCJA during the three months ended December&nbsp;31, 2017. As of
December&nbsp;31, 2017, we have not completed our accounting for the tax effects of TCJA. Our net charge is provisional based on reasonable estimates for those tax effects. Changes to these estimates or new guidance issued by regulators may
materially impact our provision for income taxes and effective tax rate in the period in which the adjustments are made. Our accounting for the tax effects of TCJA will be completed during the measurement period, which should not extend beyond the
second fiscal quarter of 2019. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">We have provided <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures related to TCJA to
aid investors in better understanding our performance. We believe these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures aid investors by providing additional insight into our operational performance and help clarify trends affecting our
business. For comparability of reporting, management considers <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures in conjunction with GAAP financial results in evaluating business performance. The
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures presented in this release should not be considered as a substitute for, or superior to, the measures of financial performance prepared in accordance with GAAP. </FONT></P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>New Accounting Standards </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">We adopted new accounting standards related to revenue recognition and leases effective July&nbsp;1, 2017. The prior periods presented here have
been restated to reflect adoption of these new standards. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Constant Currency </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Microsoft presents constant currency information to provide a framework for assessing how our underlying businesses performed excluding the effect
of foreign currency rate fluctuations. To present this information, current and comparative prior period results for entities reporting in currencies other than United States dollars are converted into United States dollars using the average
exchange rates from the comparative period rather than the actual exchange rates in effect during the respective periods. All growth comparisons relate to the corresponding period in the last fiscal year. Microsoft has provided this <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial information to aid investors in better understanding the company&#146;s performance. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures presented in this release should not be
considered as a substitute for, or superior to, the measures of financial performance prepared in accordance with GAAP. </FONT></P>
</DIV></Center>
